   21   /*
   22    * SPECGRAM Calculate spectrogram from signal.
   23    *    B = SPECGRAM(A,NFFT,Fs,WINDOW,NOVERLAP) calculates the spectrogram for
   24    *    the signal in vector A.  SPECGRAM splits the signal into overlapping
   25    *    segments, windows each with the WINDOW vector and forms the columns of
   26    *    B with their zero-padded, length NFFT discrete Fourier transforms.  Thus
   27    *    each column of B contains an estimate of the short-term, time-localized
   28    *    frequency content of the signal A.  Time increases linearly across the
   29    *    columns of B, from left to right.  Frequency increases linearly down
   30    *    the rows, starting at 0.  If A is a length NX complex signal, B is a
   31    *    complex matrix with NFFT rows and
   32    *         k = fix((NX-NOVERLAP)/(length(WINDOW)-NOVERLAP))
   33    *    columns.  If A is real, B still has k columns but the higher frequency
   34    *    components are truncated (because they are redundant); in that case,
   35    *    SPECGRAM returns B with NFFT/2+1 rows for NFFT even and (NFFT+1)/2 rows
   36    *    for NFFT odd.  If you specify a scalar for WINDOW, SPECGRAM uses a
   37    *    Hanning window of that length.  WINDOW must have length smaller than
   38    *    or equal to NFFT and greater than NOVERLAP.  NOVERLAP is the number of
   39    *    samples the sections of A overlap.  Fs is the sampling frequency
   40    *    which does not effect the spectrogram but is used for scaling plots.
   41    *
   42    *    [B,F,T] = SPECGRAM(A,NFFT,Fs,WINDOW,NOVERLAP) returns a column of
   43    *    frequencies F and one of times T at which the spectrogram is computed.
   44    *    F has length equal to the number of rows of B, T has length k. If you
   45    *    leave Fs unspecified, SPECGRAM assumes a default of 2 Hz.
   46    *
   47    *    B = SPECGRAM(A) produces the spectrogram of the signal A using default
   48    *    settings; the defaults are NFFT = minimum of 256 and the length of A, a
   49    *    Hanning window of length NFFT, and NOVERLAP = length(WINDOW)/2.  You
   50    *    can tell SPECGRAM to use the default for any parameter by leaving it
   51    *    off or using [] for that parameter, e.g. SPECGRAM(A,[],1000)
   52    *
   53    *    SPECGRAM with no output arguments plots the absolute value of the
   54    *    spectrogram in the current figure, using IMAGESC(T,F,20*log10(ABS(B))),
   55    *    AXIS XY, COLORMAP(JET) so the low frequency content of the first
   56    *    portion of the signal is displayed in the lower left corner of the axes.
   57    *
   58    *    SPECGRAM(A,F,Fs,WINDOW) where F is a vector of frequencies in Hz
   59    *    (with 2 or more elements) computes the spectrogram at those frequencies
   60    *    using either the chirp z-transform for more than 20 evenly spaced
   61    *    frequencies or a polyphase decimation filterbank.
   62    *
   63    *    See also PWELCH, CSD, COHERE and TFE.
   64    * Arguments    : emxArray_real_T *x
   65    *                double window
   66    *                double noverlap
   67    *                emxArray_creal_T *yo
   68    * Return Type  : void
   69    */

 2849     istart = b_window->size[0];
 2850     nwind = b_window->size[0];
 2851     if (x->size[1] < b_window->size[0]) {
 2852       /*  zero-pad x if it has length less than the window length */
 2853       x->data[b_window->size[0] - 1] = 0.0;
 2854       nx = b_window->size[0];
 2855     }
 2856   
 2857     emxInit_real_T1(&b_x, 1);
 2858     ihi = b_x->size[0];
 2859     b_x->size[0] = x->size[1];
 2860     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_x, ihi, (int)sizeof(double));
 2861     apnd = x->size[1];
 2862     for (ihi = 0; ihi < apnd; ihi++) {
 2863       b_x->data[ihi] = x->data[ihi];
 2864     }
 2865   
 2866     /*  make a column vector for ease later */
 2867     nm1d2 = b_window->size[0];
 2868     ihi = b_window->size[0];
 2869     b_window->size[0] = nm1d2;
 2870     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_window, ihi, (int)sizeof(double));
 2871   
 2872     /*  be consistent with data set */
 2873     ncol = ((double)nx - noverlap) / ((double)istart - noverlap);
 2874     b_fix(&ncol);
 2875     if (rtIsNaN(ncol - 1.0)) {
 2876       cdiff = 1;
 2877       twid_re = rtNaN;
 2878       b_apnd = ncol - 1.0;
 2879     } else if (ncol - 1.0 < 0.0) {
 2880       cdiff = 0;
 2881       twid_re = 0.0;
 2882       b_apnd = ncol - 1.0;
 2883     } else if (rtIsInf(ncol - 1.0)) {
 2884       cdiff = 1;
 2885       twid_re = rtNaN;
 2886       b_apnd = ncol - 1.0;
 2887     } else {
 2888       twid_re = 0.0;
 2889       ndbl = floor((ncol - 1.0) + 0.5);
 2890       b_apnd = ndbl;
 2891       b_cdiff = ndbl - (ncol - 1.0);
 2892       if (fabs(b_cdiff) < 4.4408920985006262E-16 * fabs(ncol - 1.0)) {
 2893         ndbl++;
 2894         b_apnd = ncol - 1.0;
 2895       } else if (b_cdiff > 0.0) {
 2896         b_apnd = ndbl - 1.0;
 2897       } else {
 2898         ndbl++;
 2899       }
 2900   
 2901       if (ndbl >= 0.0) {
 2902         cdiff = (int)ndbl;
 2903       } else {
 2904         cdiff = 0;
 2905       }
 2906     }
 2907   
 2908     emxInit_real_T(&colindex, 2);
 2909     ihi = colindex->size[0] * colindex->size[1];
 2910     colindex->size[0] = 1;
 2911     colindex->size[1] = cdiff;
 2912     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)colindex, ihi, (int)sizeof(double));
 2913     if (cdiff > 0) {
 2914       colindex->data[0] = twid_re;
 2915       if (cdiff > 1) {
 2916         colindex->data[cdiff - 1] = b_apnd;
 2917         ihi = cdiff - 1;
 2918         nm1d2 = ihi / 2;
 2919         for (k = 1; k < nm1d2; k++) {
 2920           colindex->data[k] = twid_re + (double)k;
 2921           colindex->data[(cdiff - k) - 1] = b_apnd - (double)k;
 2922         }
 2923   
 2924         if (nm1d2 << 1 == cdiff - 1) {
 2925           colindex->data[nm1d2] = (twid_re + b_apnd) / 2.0;
 2926         } else {
 2927           colindex->data[nm1d2] = twid_re + (double)nm1d2;
 2928           colindex->data[nm1d2 + 1] = b_apnd - (double)nm1d2;
 2929         }
 2930       }
 2931     }
 2932   
 2933     twid_re = (double)istart - noverlap;
 2934     ihi = colindex->size[0] * colindex->size[1];
 2935     colindex->size[0] = 1;
 2936     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)colindex, ihi, (int)sizeof(double));
 2937     nm1d2 = colindex->size[0];
 2938     cdiff = colindex->size[1];
 2939     apnd = nm1d2 * cdiff;
 2940     for (ihi = 0; ihi < apnd; ihi++) {
 2941       colindex->data[ihi] = 1.0 + colindex->data[ihi] * twid_re;
 2942     }
 2943   
 2944     if (istart < 1) {
 2945       cdiff = 0;
 2946       apnd = 0;
 2947     } else {
 2948       nm1d2 = (int)floor(((double)nwind - 1.0) + 0.5);
 2949       apnd = nm1d2 + 1;
 2950       cdiff = (nm1d2 - istart) + 1;
 2951       if (fabs(cdiff) < 4.4408920985006262E-16 * (double)istart) {
 2952         nm1d2++;
 2953         apnd = istart;
 2954       } else if (cdiff > 0) {
 2955         apnd = nm1d2;
 2956       } else {
 2957         nm1d2++;
 2958       }
 2959   
 2960       if (nm1d2 >= 0) {
 2961         cdiff = nm1d2;
 2962       } else {
 2963         cdiff = 0;
 2964       }
 2965     }
 2966   
 2967     emxInit_real_T(&y, 2);
 2968     ihi = y->size[0] * y->size[1];
 2969     y->size[0] = 1;
 2970     y->size[1] = cdiff;
 2971     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)y, ihi, (int)sizeof(double));
 2972     if (cdiff > 0) {
 2973       y->data[0] = 1.0;
 2974       if (cdiff > 1) {
 2975         y->data[cdiff - 1] = apnd;
 2976         ihi = cdiff - 1;
 2977         nm1d2 = ihi / 2;
 2978         for (k = 1; k < nm1d2; k++) {
 2979           y->data[k] = 1.0 + (double)k;
 2980           y->data[(cdiff - k) - 1] = apnd - k;
 2981         }
 2982   
 2983         if (nm1d2 << 1 == cdiff - 1) {
 2984           y->data[nm1d2] = (1.0 + (double)apnd) / 2.0;
 2985         } else {
 2986           y->data[nm1d2] = 1.0 + (double)nm1d2;
 2987           y->data[nm1d2 + 1] = apnd - nm1d2;
 2988         }
 2989       }
 2990     }
 2991   
 2992     emxInit_real_T1(&rowindex, 1);
 2993     ihi = rowindex->size[0];
 2994     rowindex->size[0] = y->size[1];
 2995     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)rowindex, ihi, (int)sizeof(double));
 2996     apnd = y->size[1];
 2997     for (ihi = 0; ihi < apnd; ihi++) {
 2998       rowindex->data[ihi] = y->data[y->size[0] * ihi];
 2999     }
 3000   
 3001     emxFree_real_T(&y);
 3002     nm1d2 = x->size[1];
 3003     if (nm1d2 < ((double)istart + colindex->data[(int)ncol - 1]) - 1.0) {
 3004       b_x->data[(int)(((double)istart + colindex->data[(int)ncol - 1]) - 1.0) - 1]
 3005         = 0.0;
 3006   
 3007       /*  zero-pad x */
 3008     }
 3009   
 3010     emxInit_real_T(&r2, 2);
 3011   
 3012     /*  put x into columns of y with the proper offset */
 3013     /*  should be able to do this with fancy indexing! */
 3014     apnd = rowindex->size[0];
 3015     ihi = r2->size[0] * r2->size[1];
 3016     r2->size[0] = apnd;
 3017     r2->size[1] = (int)ncol;
 3018     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)r2, ihi, (int)sizeof(double));
 3019     nm1d2 = (int)ncol;
 3020     for (ihi = 0; ihi < nm1d2; ihi++) {
 3021       for (cdiff = 0; cdiff < apnd; cdiff++) {
 3022         r2->data[cdiff + r2->size[0] * ihi] = b_x->data[(int)((rowindex->
 3023           data[cdiff] + colindex->data[colindex->size[0] * ihi]) - 1.0) - 1];
 3024       }
 3025     }
 3026   
 3027     emxFree_real_T(&rowindex);
 3028     emxFree_real_T(&colindex);
 3029     emxInit_creal_T(&b_y, 2);
 3030   
 3031     /*  Apply the window to the array of offset signal segments. */
 3032     apnd = b_window->size[0];
 3033     ihi = b_y->size[0] * b_y->size[1];
 3034     b_y->size[0] = apnd;
 3035     b_y->size[1] = (int)ncol;
 3036     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_y, ihi, (int)sizeof(creal_T));
 3037     nm1d2 = (int)ncol;
 3038     for (ihi = 0; ihi < nm1d2; ihi++) {
 3039       for (cdiff = 0; cdiff < apnd; cdiff++) {
 3040         twid_re = r2->data[cdiff + r2->size[0] * ihi];
 3041         b_y->data[cdiff + b_y->size[0] * ihi].re = b_window->data[cdiff] * twid_re;
 3042         b_y->data[cdiff + b_y->size[0] * ihi].im = b_window->data[cdiff] * 0.0;
 3043       }
 3044     }
 3045   
 3046     emxFree_real_T(&r2);
 3047     emxFree_real_T(&b_window);
 3048     emxInit_creal_T(&c_y, 2);
 3049   
 3050     /*  USE FFT */
 3051     /*  now fft y which does the columns */
 3052     ihi = c_y->size[0] * c_y->size[1];
 3053     c_y->size[0] = 8192;
 3054     c_y->size[1] = b_y->size[1];
 3055     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)c_y, ihi, (int)sizeof(creal_T));
 3056     if (8192 > b_y->size[0]) {
 3057       ihi = c_y->size[0] * c_y->size[1];
 3058       c_y->size[0] = 8192;
 3059       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)c_y, ihi, (int)sizeof(creal_T));
 3060       apnd = c_y->size[1];
 3061       for (ihi = 0; ihi < apnd; ihi++) {
 3062         for (cdiff = 0; cdiff < 8192; cdiff++) {
 3063           c_y->data[cdiff + c_y->size[0] * ihi].re = 0.0;
 3064           c_y->data[cdiff + c_y->size[0] * ihi].im = 0.0;
 3065         }
 3066       }
 3067     }
 3068   
 3069     if ((b_y->size[0] == 0) || (b_y->size[1] == 0)) {
 3070     } else {
 3071       if (b_y->size[0] <= 8192) {
 3072         minval = b_y->size[0] - 1;
 3073       } else {
 3074         minval = 8191;
 3075       }
 3076   
 3077       nm1d2 = b_y->size[0] - minval;
 3078       if (1 >= nm1d2) {
 3079         ixDelta = 1;
 3080       } else {
 3081         ixDelta = nm1d2;
 3082       }
 3083   
 3084       lastChan = (div_s32(b_y->size[0] * b_y->size[1], b_y->size[0]) - 1) << 13;
 3085       ix = 0;
 3086       for (chanStart = 0; chanStart <= lastChan; chanStart += 8192) {
 3087         nm1d2 = 0;
 3088         cdiff = chanStart;
 3089         for (i = 1; i <= minval; i++) {
 3090           c_y->data[cdiff] = b_y->data[ix];
 3091           cdiff = 8192;
 3092           tst = true;
 3093           while (tst) {
 3094             cdiff >>= 1;
 3095             nm1d2 ^= cdiff;
 3096             tst = ((nm1d2 & cdiff) == 0);
 3097           }
 3098   
 3099           cdiff = chanStart + nm1d2;
 3100           ix++;
 3101         }
 3102   
 3103         c_y->data[cdiff] = b_y->data[ix];
 3104         ix += ixDelta;
 3105         for (i = chanStart; i <= chanStart + 8190; i += 2) {
 3106           b_apnd = c_y->data[i + 1].re;
 3107           b_cdiff = c_y->data[i + 1].im;
 3108           c_y->data[i + 1].re = c_y->data[i].re - c_y->data[i + 1].re;
 3109           c_y->data[i + 1].im = c_y->data[i].im - c_y->data[i + 1].im;
 3110           c_y->data[i].re += b_apnd;
 3111           c_y->data[i].im += b_cdiff;
 3112         }
 3113   
 3114         cdiff = 2;
 3115         nm1d2 = 4;
 3116         k = 2048;
 3117         apnd = 8189;
 3118         while (k > 0) {
 3119           i = chanStart;
 3120           ihi = chanStart + apnd;
 3121           while (i < ihi) {
 3122             b_apnd = c_y->data[i + cdiff].re;
 3123             b_cdiff = c_y->data[i + cdiff].im;
 3124             c_y->data[i + cdiff].re = c_y->data[i].re - b_apnd;
 3125             c_y->data[i + cdiff].im = c_y->data[i].im - b_cdiff;
 3126             c_y->data[i].re += b_apnd;
 3127             c_y->data[i].im += b_cdiff;
 3128             i += nm1d2;
 3129           }
 3130   
 3131           istart = chanStart + 1;
 3132           for (j = k; j < 4096; j += k) {
 3133             twid_re = dv5[j];
 3134             ndbl = dv6[j];
 3135             i = istart;
 3136             ihi = istart + apnd;
 3137             while (i < ihi) {
 3138               b_apnd = twid_re * c_y->data[i + cdiff].re - ndbl * c_y->data[i +
 3139                 cdiff].im;
 3140               b_cdiff = twid_re * c_y->data[i + cdiff].im + ndbl * c_y->data[i +
 3141                 cdiff].re;
 3142               c_y->data[i + cdiff].re = c_y->data[i].re - b_apnd;
 3143               c_y->data[i + cdiff].im = c_y->data[i].im - b_cdiff;
 3144               c_y->data[i].re += b_apnd;
 3145               c_y->data[i].im += b_cdiff;
 3146               i += nm1d2;
 3147             }
 3148   
 3149             istart++;
 3150           }
 3151   
 3152           k /= 2;
 3153           cdiff = nm1d2;
 3154           nm1d2 <<= 1;
 3155           apnd -= cdiff;
 3156         }
 3157       }
 3158     }
 3159   
 3160     ihi = b_y->size[0] * b_y->size[1];
 3161     b_y->size[0] = 8192;
 3162     b_y->size[1] = c_y->size[1];
 3163     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_y, ihi, (int)sizeof(creal_T));
 3164     apnd = c_y->size[0] * c_y->size[1];
 3165     for (ihi = 0; ihi < apnd; ihi++) {
 3166       b_y->data[ihi] = c_y->data[ihi];
 3167     }
 3168   
 3169     emxInit_real_T1(&c_x, 1);
 3170     ihi = c_x->size[0];
 3171     c_x->size[0] = b_x->size[0];
 3172     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)c_x, ihi, (int)sizeof(double));
 3173     apnd = b_x->size[0];
 3174     for (ihi = 0; ihi < apnd; ihi++) {
 3175       c_x->data[ihi] = 0.0;
 3176     }
 3177   
 3178     emxFree_real_T(&b_x);
 3179     tst = any(c_x);
 3180     emxFree_real_T(&c_x);
 3181     if (!!!tst) {
 3182       /*  x purely real */
 3183       for (ihi = 0; ihi < 4097; ihi++) {
 3184         tmp_data[ihi] = (short)(1 + ihi);
 3185       }
 3186   
 3187       apnd = c_y->size[1];
 3188       ihi = b_y->size[0] * b_y->size[1];
 3189       b_y->size[0] = 4097;
 3190       b_y->size[1] = apnd;
 3191       emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)b_y, ihi, (int)sizeof(creal_T));
 3192       for (ihi = 0; ihi < apnd; ihi++) {
 3193         for (cdiff = 0; cdiff < 4097; cdiff++) {
 3194           b_y->data[cdiff + b_y->size[0] * ihi] = c_y->data[(tmp_data[cdiff] +
 3195             c_y->size[0] * ihi) - 1];
 3196         }
 3197       }
 3198     }
 3199   
 3200     emxFree_creal_T(&c_y);
 3201   
 3202     /*  take abs, and use image to display results */
 3203     /*  if nargout == 0 */
 3204     /*      newplot; */
 3205     /*      if length(t)==1 */
 3206     /*          imagesc([0 1/f(2)],f,20*log10(abs(y)+eps));axis xy; colormap(jet) */
 3207     /*      else */
 3208     /*          imagesc(t,f,20*log10(abs(y)+eps));axis xy; colormap(jet) */
 3209     /*      end */
 3210     /*      xlabel('Time') */
 3211     /*      ylabel('Frequency') */
 3212     ihi = yo->size[0] * yo->size[1];
 3213     yo->size[0] = b_y->size[0];
 3214     yo->size[1] = b_y->size[1];
 3215     emxEnsureCapacity((emxArray__common *)yo, ihi, (int)sizeof(creal_T));
 3216     apnd = b_y->size[0] * b_y->size[1];
 3217     for (ihi = 0; ihi < apnd; ihi++) {
 3218       yo->data[ihi] = b_y->data[ihi];
 3219     }
 3220   
 3221     emxFree_creal_T(&b_y);
 3222   
 3223     /*  function [msg,x,nfft,Fs,window,noverlap] = specgramchk(P) */
 3224     /*  %SPECGRAMCHK Helper function for SPECGRAM. */
 3225     /*  %   SPECGRAMCHK(P) takes the cell array P and uses each cell as  */
 3226     /*  %   an input argument.  Assumes P has between 1 and 5 elements. */
 3227     /*   */
 3228     /*  msg = []; */
 3229     /*   */
 3230     /*  x = P{1};  */
 3231     /*  if (length(P) > 1) & ~isempty(P{2}) */
 3232     /*      nfft = P{2}; */
 3233     /*  else */
 3234     /*      nfft = min(length(x),256); */
 3235     /*  end */
 3236     /*  if (length(P) > 2) & ~isempty(P{3}) */
 3237     /*      Fs = P{3}; */
 3238     /*  else */
 3239     /*      Fs = 2; */
 3240     /*  end */
 3241     /*  if length(P) > 3 & ~isempty(P{4}) */
 3242     /*      window = P{4};  */
 3243     /*  else */
 3244     /*      if length(nfft) == 1 */
 3245     /*          window = hanning(nfft); */
 3246     /*      else */
 3247     /*          msg = 'You must specify a window function.'; */
 3248     /*      end */
 3249     /*  end */
 3250     /*  if length(window) == 1, window = hanning(window); end */
 3251     /*  if (length(P) > 4) & ~isempty(P{5}) */
 3252     /*      noverlap = P{5}; */
 3253     /*  else */
 3254     /*      noverlap = ceil(length(window)/2); */
 3255     /*  end */
 3256     /*   */
 3257     /*  % NOW do error checking */
 3258     /*  if (length(nfft)==1) & (nfft<length(window)),  */
 3259     /*      msg = 'Requires window''s length to be no greater than the FFT length.'; */
 3260     /*  end */
 3261     /*  if (noverlap >= length(window)), */
 3262     /*      msg = 'Requires NOVERLAP to be strictly less than the window length.'; */
 3263     /*  end */
 3264     /*  if (length(nfft)==1) & (nfft ~= abs(round(nfft))) */
 3265     /*      msg = 'Requires positive integer values for NFFT.'; */
 3266     /*  end */
 3267     /*  if (noverlap ~= abs(round(noverlap))), */
 3268     /*      msg = 'Requires positive integer value for NOVERLAP.'; */
 3269     /*  end */
 3270     /*  if min(size(x))~=1, */
 3271     /*      msg = 'Requires vector (either row or column) input.'; */
 3272     /*  end */
 3273     /*  end */
 3274   }
